<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overeen.html>overeen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:equal.html>equal</a>, matching</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stemmen.html>stemmen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tune.html>tune</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:adjust.html>adjust</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
